------- FILE i2c_v2.2.inc LEVEL 3 PASS 4
      0  1e2c					      include	"i2c_v2.2.inc"
      1  1e2c							;
      2  1e2c							; i2c_v2.2.inc
      3  1e2c							;
      4  1e2c							;
      5  1e2c							; AtariVox EEPROM Driver
      6  1e2c							;
      7  1e2c							; By Alex Herbert, 2004
      8  1e2c							;
      9  1e2c							; Optimisations by Thomas Jentzsch, 2006/2008
     10  1e2c							;
     11  1e2c
     12  1e2c
     13  1e2c							; I/O Constants
     14  1e2c
     15  1e2c		       00 04	   I2C_SDA_MASK equ	$04
     16  1e2c		       00 08	   I2C_SCL_MASK equ	$08
     17  1e2c
     18  1e2c
     19  1e2c							; Signalling Macros
     20  1e2c
     21  1e2c							;  MAC     I2C_SCL_0
     22  1e2c							;    lda     #$00
     23  1e2c							;    sta     SWCHA
     24  1e2c							;  ENDM
     25  1e2c
     26  1e2c							;  MAC     I2C_SCL_1
     27  1e2c							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK
     28  1e2c							;    sta     SWCHA
     29  1e2c							;  ENDM
     30  1e2c
     31  1e2c							;  MAC     I2C_SDA_IN
     32  1e2c							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK
     33  1e2c							;    sta     SWACNT
     34  1e2c							;  ENDM
     35  1e2c
     36  1e2c							;  MAC     I2C_SDA_OUT
     37  1e2c							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
     38  1e2c							;    sta     SWACNT
     39  1e2c							;  ENDM
     40  1e2c
     41  1e2c
     42  1e2c					      MAC	i2c_start
     43  1e2c							; I2C_SCL_1
     44  1e2c					      lda	#(I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK)*2	; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     45  1e2c					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     46  1e2c							; I2C_SDA_OUT
     47  1e2c					      lsr		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
     48  1e2c					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
     49  1e2c							; total: 12 cycles
     50  1e2c					      ENDM
     51  1e2c
     52  1e2c
     53  1e2c					      MAC	i2c_txbit
     54  1e2c							; I2C_SCL_0
     55  1e2c					      lda	#%0011	; 2
     56  1e2c					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     57  1e2c							; set bit
     58  1e2c					      adc	#%1000	; 2
     59  1e2c					      sta	SWACNT	; 4	     SDA = !C (a = %1000 / %1100)
     60  1e2c							; I2C_SCL_1
     61  1e2c					      lda	#I2C_SCL_MASK	; 2
     62  1e2c					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     63  1e2c							; total: 18 cycles
     64  1e2c					      ENDM
     65  1e2c
     66  1e2c
     67  1e2c					      MAC	i2c_txnack
     68  1e2c							; I2C_SCL_0
     69  1e2c					      lda	#I2C_SCL_MASK*2	; 2	     $00
     70  1e2c					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     71  1e2c							; I2C_SDA_IN
     72  1e2c					      lsr		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     73  1e2c					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
     74  1e2c							; I2C_SCL_1
     75  1e2c					      nop		; 2	     required for timing!
     76  1e2c					      sta	SWCHA	; 4	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     77  1e2c							; total: 18 cycles
     78  1e2c					      ENDM
     79  1e2c
     80  1e2c
     81  1e2c							; Subroutine Macros
     82  1e2c
     83  1e2c					      MAC	i2c_subs
     84  1e2c
     85  1e2c				   i2c_startread
     86  1e2c							; use V to flag if previous byte needs ACK
     87  1e2c					      ldy	#%10100001	; 2	     eeprom read command
     88  1e2c					      .byte	$2c	; 2
     89  1e2c				   i2c_startwrite
     90  1e2c					      ldy	#%10100000	; 2	     eeprom write command
     91  1e2c					      I2C_START		;12	     start signal (clears V flag)
     92  1e2c					      tya		; 2 = 16
     93  1e2c				   i2c_txbyte
     94  1e2c					      eor	#$ff	; 2	     invert data byte
     95  1e2c					      sec		; 2
     96  1e2c					      rol		; 2 =	6    shift loop bit into a
     97  1e2c				   i2c_txbyteloop
     98  1e2c					      tay		; 2
     99  1e2c					      I2C_TXBIT		;18	     transmit
    100  1e2c					      tya		; 2
    101  1e2c					      asl		; 2	     shift next bit into C
    102  1e2c					      bne	i2c_txbyteloop	; 2= 26/27
    103  1e2c
    104  1e2c							; receive acknowledge bit
    105  1e2c
    106  1e2c					      beq	i2c_rxbit	;43 = 43
    107  1e2c							; i2c_txbyte: 264 cycles
    108  1e2c							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    109  1e2c
    110  1e2c				   i2c_rxbyte
    111  1e2c					      bvc	i2c_rxskipack	; 2	     previous byte needs acknowledge?
    112  1e2c					      jsr	i2c_txack	;24	     transmit acknowledge bit
    113  1e2c
    114  1e2c				   i2c_rxskipack
    115  1e2c					      bit	i2c_rxbyte	; 4	     set V - next byte(s) require acknowledge
    116  1e2c
    117  1e2c					      lda	#1	; 2
    118  1e2c				   i2c_rxbyteloop
    119  1e2c					      tay		; 2 =	2
    120  1e2c				   i2c_rxbit		;	     receive bit in C
    121  1e2c					      I2C_TXNACK		;18 = 18
    122  1e2c
    123  1e2c					      lda	SWCHA	; 4
    124  1e2c					      lsr		; 2
    125  1e2c					      lsr		; 2
    126  1e2c					      lsr		; 2 = 10    C = SDA
    127  1e2c
    128  1e2c					      tya		; 2
    129  1e2c					      rol		; 2	     rotate into Y
    130  1e2c					      bcc	i2c_rxbyteloop	; 2=	6/7
    131  1e2c
    132  1e2c							; received byte in A
    133  1e2c					      rts		; 6 =	6
    134  1e2c							; i2c_rxbit:  40 cycles
    135  1e2c							; i2c_rxbyte: 310/333 cycles
    136  1e2c							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    137  1e2c
    138  1e2c				   i2c_stopread
    139  1e2c					      bvc	i2c_stopwrite	; 2
    140  1e2c					      ldy	#$80	; 2
    141  1e2c					      jsr	i2c_rxbit	;46	     transmit no-acknowledge
    142  1e2c
    143  1e2c				   i2c_stopwrite
    144  1e2c					      jsr	i2c_txack	;30
    145  1e2c
    146  1e2c							; return port to input mode
    147  1e2c					      lda	#0	; 2	     0
    148  1e2c					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
    149  1e2c					      rts		; 6 = 12
    150  1e2c							; i2c_stopread:  45/92
    151  1e2c							; i2c_stopwrite: 42
    152  1e2c							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    153  1e2c
    154  1e2c				   i2c_txack
    155  1e2c							; I2C_SCL_0
    156  1e2c					      lda	#0	; 2	     $00
    157  1e2c					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
    158  1e2c							; I2C_SDA_OUT
    159  1e2c					      lda	#(I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK)	; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
    160  1e2c					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
    161  1e2c							; I2C_SCL_1
    162  1e2c					      asl		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
    163  1e2c					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
    164  1e2c
    165  1e2c					      rts		; 6
    166  1e2c							; total: 24 cycles
    167  1e2c							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    168  1e2c
    169  1e2c					      ENDM
    170  1e2c
    171  1e2c
    172  1e2c

    672  1e97

      1  1e97		       00 03	   BANK_ReadSaveKey =	_CURRENT_BANK

      3  1e97				   ReadSaveKey
    675  1e97
    676  1e97							; assume no SaveKey found:
    677  1e97		       a9 ff		      lda	#$ff	; 2	     return $ff if no SaveKey found
    678  1e99		       85 df		      sta	highScoreSK+2	; 3
    679  1e9b
    680  1e9b							; setup SaveKey:
    681  1e9b		       a5 e0		      lda	startingLevel	; 3	     load start levelX*5 and level
    682  1e9d		       a6 b5		      ldx	level	; 3
    683  1e9f		       20 d8 f6 	      jsr	SetupSaveKey	;6+853
    684  1ea2		       90 52		      bcc	NoSKfound	; 2/3
    685  1ea4
    686  1ea4							;    lda     #$34
    687  1ea4							;    sta     COLUBK
    688  1ea4
    689  1ea4							; start read
    690  1ea4		       20 7f f6 	      jsr	i2c_stopwrite	;6+42	     end of "fake" write
    691  1ea7		       20 2c f6 	      jsr	i2c_startread	;6+284      Start signal and $a1 command byte
    692  1eaa
    693  1eaa							; read high score:
    694  1eaa		       a2 02		      ldx	#3-1	; 2 = 1187
    695  1eac				   .loopRead
    696  1eac		       20 55 f6 	      jsr	i2c_rxbyte	;6+333      read byte from EEPROM
    697  1eaf		       c9 ff		      cmp	#$ff	; 2	     EEPROM slot empty?
    698  1eb1		       d0 02		      bne	.skipEmpty	; 2/3	      no, skip clear
    699  1eb3		       a9 00		      lda	#0	; 2	     clear EEPROM slot
    700  1eb5				   .skipEmpty
    701  1eb5		       95 dd		      sta	highScoreSK,x	; 4
    702  1eb7		       ca		      dex		; 2
    703  1eb8		       10 f2		      bpl	.loopRead	; 2/3= 354
    704  1eba
    705  1eba							; stop read:
    706  1eba		       4c 78 f6 	      jmp	i2c_stopread	;3+92=95    terminate read
    707  1ebd

      2  1ebd					      SUBROUTINE
      3  1ebd				   WriteSaveKey
    710  1ebd
    711  1ebd							; check if new high score:

    713  1ebf		       e8		      inx		; 2

    715  1ec2

    718  1ec4		       a6 e1		      ldx	startLevel	; 3

      3  1ed8				   SetupSaveKey
    739  1ed8
    740  1ed8							; calculate slot;
    741  1ed8							; a = levelX
    742  1ed8							; x = level (0..4)
    743  1ed8		       85 e2		      sta	offsetSK	; 3
    744  1eda		       8a		      txa		; 2
    745  1edb		       18		      clc		; 2
    746  1edc		       65 e2		      adc	offsetSK	; 3
    747  1ede		       85 e2		      sta	offsetSK	; 3
    748  1ee0		       0a		      asl		; 2	     multiply by 3
    749  1ee1		       65 e2		      adc	offsetSK	; 3
    750  1ee3		       69 00		      adc	#<SAVEKEY_ADR	; 2
    751  1ee5		       aa		      tax		; 2 = 22
    752  1ee6							; detect SaveKey:
    753  1ee6		       20 2f f6 	      jsr	i2c_startwrite	;6+280
    754  1ee9		       d0 0a		      bne	.exitSK	; 2/3
    755  1eeb

    757  1eeb		       b8		      clv		; 2
    758  1eec		       a9 2f		      lda	#>SAVEKEY_ADR	; 2	     upper byte of address
    759  1eee		       20 3b f6 	      jsr	i2c_txbyte	;6+264
    760  1ef1		       8a		      txa		; 2	     x = lower byte offset
    761  1ef2		       4c 3b f6 	      jmp	i2c_txbyte	;3+264      returns C==1
    762  1ef5
    763  1ef5				   .exitSK
    764  1ef5		       18		      clc
    765  1ef6				   NoSKfound
    766  1ef6		       60		      rts

      2  37e2					      ECHO	"LEVELS3 -- full 2K", "(2K) SIZE = ", .TEMP, ", FREE=", ROM_BANK_SIZE - .TEMP

    188  4db3							;Player	@	0x40
    189  4db3							;Player on goal square	+	0x2b
    190  4db3							;Box	$	0x24
    191  4db3							;Box on goal square	*	0x2a
    192  4db3							;Goal square	.	0x2e
    193  4db3							;Floor	(Space)	0x20 or underscore
    194  4db3
    195  4db3							;This level ("Claire", by Lee J Haywood):
    196  4db3
    197  4db3							;#######
    198  4db3							;#.@ # #
    199  4db3							;#$* $ #
    200  4db3							;#   $ #
    201  4db3							;# ..	#
    202  4db3							;#  *	#
    203  4db3							;#######
    204  4db3							;runlength encoded looks like this:
    205  4db3
    206  4db3							;The rows of the level are separated by "|"s. There has been a discussion in the Yahoo Group about what character should represent an empty square in May 2006. Finally the hyphen has been elected to be the standard character for an empty square. Nevertheless, programs are encouraged to support both, hyphens and underscores.

 LEVELS6 -- full 2K (2K) SIZE =  $5b3 , FREE= $24d
      2  4db3					      ECHO	"LEVELS6 -- full 2K", "(2K) SIZE = ", .TEMP, ", FREE=", ROM_BANK_SIZE - .TEMP
      3  4db3				  -	      if	( .TEMP ) > ROM_BANK_SIZE
      4  4db3				  -	      ECHO	"BANK OVERFLOW @ ", * - ORIGIN
      5  4db3				  -	      ERR
      6  4db3					      endif

      0  5845					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	CopyROMShadowToRAM	; in INITBANK
      1  5845		       00 0b	   BANK_CopyROMShadowToRAM =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  5845					      SUBROUTINE
      3  5845				   CopyROMShadowToRAM
    117  5845
    118  5845							; Function copies a RAM prototype ROM bank into the destination RAM bank.  Typically
    119  5845							; the variable definitions are in the ROM shadow because this allows auto-initialisation
    120  5845							; of the variable contents from ROM declarations, but still allows access to them as
    121  5845							; variables when the correct RAM bank is switched in.	Code is also, of course, copied
    122  5845							; into the RAM destination so that code is callable whenever the ROM *or* RAM bank is
    123  5845							; switched in.  Further, if multiple copies are made to multiple RAM banks, then the
    124  5845							; code co-lives in all banks and may run even as bankswitching occurs between those
    125  5845							; banks -- by the very code itself.
    126  5845
    127  5845							; Note: Relies on ROM_Bank having being set via CALL mechanism to call this function
    128  5845		       85 c1		      sta	Board_AddressR+1
    129  5847		       86 db		      stx	O_ROM_Source_Bank	; source bank
    130  5849		       84 c5		      sty	RAM_Bank	; destination bank
    131  584b
    132  584b		       a0 00		      ldy	#0
    133  584d		       84 c0		      sty	Board_AddressR
    134  584f		       84 c2		      sty	Board_AddressW
    135  5851		       a9 14		      lda	#>($1000+RAM_WRITE)
    136  5853		       85 c3		      sta	Board_AddressW+1
    137  5855
    138  5855							; Iterate 4 pages (1K) for complete bank copy
    139  5855
    140  5855		       a9 04		      lda	#4
    141  5857		       85 da		      sta	O_CopyCount
    142  5859
    143  5859		       84 dc	   CopyPage   sty	O_Index
    144  585b		       a5 db		      lda	O_ROM_Source_Bank
    145  585d		       20 0f f8 	      jsr	GetROMByte	; get byte from ROM shadow bank
    146  5860							;tax
    147  5860		       a4 dc		      ldy	O_Index
    148  5862		       a6 c5		      ldx	RAM_Bank
    149  5864		       20 1d f8 	      jsr	PutBoardCharacter	;6+21(A)	 write byte to RAM bank
    150  5867
    151  5867		       a4 dc		      ldy	O_Index
    152  5869		       c8		      iny
    153  586a		       d0 ed		      bne	CopyPage
    154  586c
    155  586c		       e6 c1		      inc	Board_AddressR+1
    156  586e		       e6 c3		      inc	Board_AddressW+1
    157  5870
    158  5870		       c6 da		      dec	O_CopyCount
    159  5872		       d0 e5		      bne	CopyPage
    160  5874
    161  5874		       a4 c5		      ldy	RAM_Bank	; TODO: remove!?
    162  5876		       60		      rts
    163  5877

      0  5877					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	SetPlatformColours	; in INITBANK

      3  5877				   SetPlatformColours
    167  5877
    168  5877							; Now modify the hardwired colours so that we're correctly switched for NTSC/PAL
    169  5877							; The platform (0=NTSC, 1=PAL) is set from the right difficulty switch
    170  5877							; Note: This relies on DrawTheScreen starting on page boundary so that the (),y
    171  5877							; addressing will not violate the page-crossing restriction of 3E.

    174  5877

    215  58b4

      0  780f					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	GetROMByte	;=23(A)
      1  780f		       00 0f	   BANK_GetROMByte =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  780f					      SUBROUTINE
      3  780f				   GetROMByte
     61  780f
     62  780f							; a = ROM bank to retrieve
     63  780f							; y = page index
     64  780f							; ROM_Bank = bank to return to
     65  780f							; (Board_AddressR) = page
     66  780f							; out a = byte from (Board_AddressR)
     67  780f
     68  780f		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK	;3
     69  7811		       4c 16 f8 	      jmp	GetBoardCharacter2	;3+17(A)	 unconditional
     70  7814

     72  7814
      0  7814					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	GetBoardCharacter	;=20(A)
      1  7814		       00 0f	   BANK_GetBoardCharacter =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  7814					      SUBROUTINE
      3  7814				   GetBoardCharacter
     74  7814
     75  7814							; call from ROM bank
     76  7814							; switches back to ROM_Bank on exit
     77  7814
     78  7814							; pass A = bank containing character
     79  7814							; Y = x character position
     80  7814							; (Board_AddressR) points to character position
     81  7814							; returns character from board
     82  7814
     83  7814
     84  7814		       85 3e		      sta	SET_BANK_RAM	;3   switch to bank to read
     85  7816
     86  7816				   GetBoardCharacter2		;=17(A)
     87  7816
     88  7816		       b3 c0		      lax	(Board_AddressR),y	;5

      0  789b					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	SwitchObjects	;=72
      1  789b		       00 0f	   BANK_SwitchObjects =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  789b					      SUBROUTINE
      3  789b				   SwitchObjects
    224  789b
    225  789b							; The game loop has come to an end. The only possible "still happening" thing is the sort, which runs
    226  789b							; in parallel with other processes (objects, draw stack, etc). We may or may not want to wait for the
    227  789b							; sort to complete.  This code does all the checks needed to switch to the next game frame.
    228  789b
    229  789b		       ad 84 02 	      lda	INTIM	; 4
    230  789e		       c9 02		      cmp	#SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS	; 2
    231  78a0		       90 f8		      bcc	EarlyAbort	; 2/3= 8
      0  78a2					      STRESS_TIME	SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS
      1  78a2				  -	      IF	TEST_SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS = 1
      2  78a2				  -
      3  78a2				  -
      4  78a2				  -
      5  78a2				  -
      6  78a2				  -
      7  78a2				  -	      echo	"***** WARNING! STRESS_TIME enabled @", ., "! *****"
      8  78a2				  -	      bne	. - 7
      9  78a2					      ENDIF
    233  78a2
    234  78a2							; If we're undertime, then abort. The sort will continue to run, and that's great. Only when
    235  78a2							; we're at the throttle cutoff do we switch game-frames.
    236  78a2
    237  78a2							;sec
    238  78a2		       a5 b7		      lda	Throttle	;3
    239  78a4		       e9 a0		      sbc	#MAX_THROTTLE	;2
    240  78a6		       90 f2		      bcc	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 plenty of time left!
    241  78a8
    242  78a8							; Time is up. But we may be in a level which requires perfect sorting
    243  78a8							; So we check for these levels, and wait for the sort to complete for those.
    244  78a8
    245  78a8		       24 b6		      bit	levelDisplay	;3
    246  78aa		       50 08		      bvc	keepFractional	;2/3		 screen does not require complete sort
    247  78ac
    248  78ac							; We have a level which requires the sort to go to completion
    249  78ac							; Check to see if the sort is finished...
    250  78ac
    251  78ac		       a4 cc		      ldy	sortPtr	;3
    252  78ae		       d0 ea		      bne	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 sort still in progress, so wait
    253  78b0		       a4 cb		      ldy	sortRequired	;3
    254  78b2		       10 e6		      bpl	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 sort still in progress, so wait
    255  78b4
    256  78b4		       85 b7	   keepFractional sta	Throttle	;3		 save fractional 'left over' bit
    257  78b6
    258  78b6							; Pause the game with B/W switch:
    259  78b6
    260  78b6		       a5 80		      lda	gameMode
    261  78b8		       30 14		      bmi	.paused	; pause flag set
    262  78ba
    263  78ba							; Now that we have completed processing the object stack, we switch
    264  78ba							; the stack bank pointers for the next time around.
    265  78ba
    266  78ba		       a5 85		      lda	ObjStackNum	;3
    267  78bc		       49 01		      eor	#1	;2
    268  78be		       aa		      tax		;2
    269  78bf		       86 85		      stx	ObjStackNum	;3		 swap stacks @here
    270  78c1
    271  78c1							; STOP the sort so it doesn't corrupt the "other" object stack. Sort may get a look-in immediately after
    272  78c1							; this code is finished, so we don't want it to do something unexpected!
    273  78c1
    274  78c1		       a0 ff		      ldy	#<(-1)	;2
    275  78c3		       84 cb		      sty	sortRequired	;3
    276  78c5		       c8		      iny		;2		 Y==0
    277  78c6		       84 cc		      sty	sortPtr	;3
    278  78c8
    279  78c8							; Initialise the iterator and stack pointer for next time around.
    280  78c8							; Previously the stack pointer auto-initialised by popping the stack. Now we have an iterator it's
    281  78c8							; necessary to initialise both.
    282  78c8
    283  78c8		       84 cd		      sty	ObjIterator	;3		 Y==0
    284  78ca		       94 86		      sty	ObjStackPtr,x	;4
    285  78cc
    286  78cc		       84 89		      sty	ScreenDrawPhase	;3
    287  78ce				   .paused
    288  78ce		       60	   quickExit  rts		;6

    469  7921
    470  7921							; IF the creature runs out of time to do stuff, then rts HOWEVER the creature must eventually do something
    471  7921							;  as it will be continually called in available time-slices until it does. This can lockup the system.

    516  794e
    517  794e							; Nice addition limits overflow of the stack, BUT always reserves a spot for the man.
    518  794e							; Objects are unceremoniously dumped when there's not enough space.  This is just trying to cater
    519  794e							; for a no-win situation. Try and preserve the player at the cost of correct gameplay. Avoid crashing.
    520  794e
    521  794e

    523  794e				  -	      cmp	#TYPE_MAN	; 2
    524  794e					      ENDIF

    529  7954				   alwaysAllowMan

      0  7a1b					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	TimeSlice
      1  7a1b		       00 0f	   BANK_TimeSlice =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  7a1b					      SUBROUTINE
      3  7a1b				   TimeSlice
    710  7a1b
    711  7a1b							; FIRST check the time is sufficient for the smallest of the timeslices. Not much point
    712  7a1b							; going ahead if there's insufficient time. This allows the previous character drawing to
    713  7a1b							; be much smaller in time, as they don't have to include the timeslice code overhead.
    714  7a1b
    715  7a1b		       ad 84 02 	      lda	INTIM	; 4
    716  7a1e		       c9 05		      cmp	#SEGTIME_MINIMUM_TIMESLICE	; 2
    717  7a20		       90 b4		      bcc	timeExit	; 2(3)
    718  7a22
    719  7a22							; Uses the phase variable to vector to the correct processing code for the given timeslice
    720  7a22							; Code may be in any bank. Avoid the fixed bank at all costs!	Once a section is complete
    721  7a22							; it should increment ScreenDrawPhase.
    722  7a22
    723  7a22							; Switched-in bank(s) are undefined after this function is called!
    724  7a22
    725  7a22		       a9 03		      lda	#BANK_TS_PhaseVectorLO	; 2
    726  7a24		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK	; 3
    727  7a26
    728  7a26		       a6 89		      ldx	ScreenDrawPhase	; 3		 current phase of drawing
    729  7a28		       bd 4f f5 	      lda	TS_PhaseVectorLO,x	; 4
    730  7a2b		       85 da		      sta	TS_Vector	; 3
    731  7a2d		       bd 54 f5 	      lda	TS_PhaseVectorHI,x	; 4
    732  7a30		       85 db		      sta	TS_Vector+1	; 3
    733  7a32
    734  7a32		       bd 59 f5 	      lda	TS_PhaseBank,x	; 4
    735  7a35		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK	; 3		 switch bank
    736  7a37
    737  7a37		       6c da 00 	      jmp	(TS_Vector)	; 3 = 40	 vector to timeslice handler
    738  7a3a
    739  7a3a							; = 55 minimum return time (if segtime abort)

    872  7ab8
    873  7ab8		       f0 00	   SEGMENT_DECODE_LEVEL_SHADOW =	$F000	; if not = $F000, this will cause an assertion failure
    874  7ab8

    876  7aba		       a0 0a		      ldy	#BANK_DECODE_LEVEL
    877  7abc		       20 95 fc 	      jsr	CopyROM2RAM_F000

------- FILE sound/intro1_player.asm LEVEL 3 PASS 4
      0  7b44					      include	"sound/intro1_player.asm"
      1  7b44							; TIATracker music player
      2  7b44							; Copyright 2016 Andre "Kylearan" Wichmann
      3  7b44							; Website: https://bitbucket.org/kylearan/tiatracker
      4  7b44							; Email: andre.wichmann@gmx.de
      5  7b44							;
      6  7b44							; Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
      7  7b44							; you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
      8  7b44							; You may obtain a copy of the License at
      9  7b44							;
     10  7b44							;   http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
     11  7b44							;
     12  7b44							; Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
     13  7b44							; distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
     14  7b44							; WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
     15  7b44							; See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
     16  7b44							; limitations under the License.
     17  7b44
     18  7b44							; Song author: 
     19  7b44							; Song name: 
     20  7b44
     21  7b44							; @com.wudsn.ide.asm.hardware=ATARI2600
     22  7b44
     23  7b44							; =====================================================================
     24  7b44							; TIATracker Player
     25  7b44							; =====================================================================
     26  7b44				   tt_PlayerStart
     27  7b44
     28  7b44							; PLANNED PLAYER VARIANTS:
     29  7b44							; - RAM, speed, player ROM: c0/c1 patterns have same length
     30  7b44							; - RAM: Pack 2 values (out of cur_pat_index, cur_note_index, envelope_index)
     31  7b44							;	 into one and use lsr/asl to unpack them, allowing only ranges of
     32  7b44							;	 16/16 or 32/8 for them, depending on number of patterns, max
     33  7b44							;	 pattern size and max ADSR size
     34  7b44							; - ROM: Check if tt_SequenceTable can hold ptrs directly without indexing
     35  7b44							;	 tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi. Can be smaller if not many patterns get repeated
     36  7b44							;	 (saves table and decode routine)
     37  7b44							; - Speed: Inline tt_CalcInsIndex
     38  7b44							; - Speed: Store ptr to current note in RAM instead of reconstructing it?
     39  7b44							;	 Might also save the need for cur_note_index
     40  7b44
     41  7b44
     42  7b44							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
     43  7b44							; Helper macro: Retrieves current note. May advance pattern if needed.
     44  7b44							; Becomes a subroutine if TT_USE_OVERLAY is used.
     45  7b44							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
     46  7b44					      MAC	tt_fetch_current_note
     47  7b44							; construct ptr to pattern
     48  7b44				   .constructPatPtr
     49  7b44					      ldy	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x	; get current pattern (index into tt_SequenceTable)
     50  7b44					      lda	tt_SequenceTable,y
     51  7b44					      IF	TT_USE_GOTO = 1
     52  7b44					      bpl	.noPatternGoto
     53  7b44					      and	#%01111111	; mask out goto bit to get pattern number
     54  7b44					      sta	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x	; store goto'ed pattern index
     55  7b44					      bpl	.constructPatPtr	; unconditional
     56  7b44				   .noPatternGoto
     57  7b44					      ENDIF
     58  7b44					      tay
     59  7b44					      lda	tt_PatternPtrLo,y
     60  7b44					      sta	tt_ptr
     61  7b44					      lda	tt_PatternPtrHi,y
     62  7b44					      sta	tt_ptr+1
     63  7b44							; get new note
     64  7b44					      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 0
     65  7b44					      ldy	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     66  7b44					      ELSE
     67  7b44							; If the V flag is set and if the new note is an instrument,
     68  7b44							; it means it got pre-fetched by an overlay percussion, it has
     69  7b44							; to remain in sustain.
     70  7b44					      clv
     71  7b44							; check if note had been pre-fetched by overlay perc already
     72  7b44					      lda	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     73  7b44					      bpl	.notPrefetched
     74  7b44							; If so, remove flag
     75  7b44					      and	#%01111111
     76  7b44					      sta	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     77  7b44							; Set V flag for later
     78  7b44					      bit	tt_Bit6Set
     79  7b44				   .notPrefetched
     80  7b44					      tay
     81  7b44					      ENDIF
     82  7b44					      lda	(tt_ptr),y
     83  7b44							; pre-process new note
     84  7b44							; 7..5: instrument (1..7), 4..0 (0..31): frequency
     85  7b44							; 0/0: End of pattern
     86  7b44					      bne	.noEndOfPattern
     87  7b44							; End of pattern: Advance to next pattern
     88  7b44					      sta	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x	; a is 0
     89  7b44					      inc	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x
     90  7b44					      bne	.constructPatPtr	; unconditional
     91  7b44				   .noEndOfPattern
     92  7b44					      ENDM
     93  7b44
     94  7b44
     95  7b44							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
     96  7b44							; Music player entry. Call once per frame.
     97  7b44							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
     98  7b44				   tt_Player  SUBROUTINE
     99  7b44							; ==================== Sequencer ====================
    100  7b44							; Decrease speed timer
    101  7b44		       c6 cf		      dec	tt_timer
    102  7b46		       10 6e		      bpl	.noNewNote
    103  7b48
    104  7b48							; Timer ran out: Do sequencer
    105  7b48							; Advance to next note
    106  7b48		       a2 01		      ldx	#1	; 2 channels
    107  7b4a				   .advanceLoop
    108  7b4a					      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 1
    109  7b4a		       20 60 fb 	      jsr	tt_FetchNote
    110  7b4d				  -	      ELSE
    111  7b4d				  -	      TT_FETCH_CURRENT_NOTE
    112  7b4d					      ENDIF
    113  7b4d							; Parse new note from pattern
    114  7b4d		       c9 10		      cmp	#TT_INS_PAUSE
    115  7b4f					      IF	TT_USE_SLIDE = 0
    116  7b4f		       90 55		      bcc	.finishedNewNote
    117  7b51		       d0 3d		      bne	.newNote
    118  7b53				  -	      ELSE
    119  7b53				  -	      beq	.pause
    120  7b53				  -	      bcs	.newNote
    121  7b53				  -
    122  7b53				  -			; --- slide/hold ---
    123  7b53				  -			; Adjust frequency and hold note in sustain.
    124  7b53				  -			; composer/tracker has to make sure that no unwanted
    125  7b53				  -			; under/overflow happens.
    126  7b53				  -			; Note: f = f + (8-(16-x)) = x + f - 8
    127  7b53				  -	      adc	tt_cur_ins_c0,x	; carry is clear after cmp
    128  7b53				  -	      sec
    129  7b53				  -	      sbc	#8
    130  7b53				  -	      sta	tt_cur_ins_c0,x
    131  7b53				  -	      bcs	.finishedNewNote	; unconditional, since legally no underflow can happen (ins>0 or HOLD for ins=0)
    132  7b53					      ENDIF
    133  7b53
    134  7b53							; --- pause ---
    135  7b53				   .pause
    136  7b53							; Get release index for current instrument. Since a pause can
    137  7b53							; only follow an instrument, we don't need to handle percussion
    138  7b53							; or commands.
    139  7b53		       b5 d6		      lda	tt_cur_ins_c0,x
    140  7b55		       20 ee fb 	      jsr	tt_CalcInsIndex
    141  7b58		       b9 ac fc 	      lda	tt_InsReleaseIndexes-1,y	; -1 b/c instruments start at #1
    142  7b5b							; Put it into release. Skip junk byte so index no longer indicates
    143  7b5b							; sustain phase.
    144  7b5b		       18		      clc
    145  7b5c		       69 01		      adc	#1
    146  7b5e		       90 44		      bcc	.storeADIndex	; unconditional
    147  7b60
    148  7b60							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    149  7b60							; Helper subroutine to minimize ROM footprint. Will be inlined if
    150  7b60							; TT_USE_OVERLAY is not used.
    151  7b60							; Interleaved here so player can be inlined.
    152  7b60							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    153  7b60					      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 1
    154  7b60				   tt_FetchNote
      0  7b60					      TT_FETCH_CURRENT_NOTE
      1  7b60
      2  7b60				   .constructPatPtr
      3  7b60		       b4 d0		      ldy	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x
      4  7b62		       b9 bf fd 	      lda	tt_SequenceTable,y
      5  7b65					      IF	TT_USE_GOTO = 1
      6  7b65		       10 06		      bpl	.noPatternGoto
      7  7b67		       29 7f		      and	#%01111111
      8  7b69		       95 d0		      sta	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x
      9  7b6b		       10 f3		      bpl	.constructPatPtr
     10  7b6d				   .noPatternGoto
     11  7b6d					      ENDIF
     12  7b6d		       a8		      tay
     13  7b6e		       b9 b5 fd 	      lda	tt_PatternPtrLo,y
     14  7b71		       85 d8		      sta	tt_ptr
     15  7b73		       b9 ba fd 	      lda	tt_PatternPtrHi,y
     16  7b76		       85 d9		      sta	tt_ptr+1
     17  7b78
     18  7b78				  -	      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 0
     19  7b78				  -	      ldy	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     20  7b78					      ELSE
     21  7b78
     22  7b78
     23  7b78
     24  7b78		       b8		      clv
     25  7b79
     26  7b79		       b5 d2		      lda	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     27  7b7b		       10 07		      bpl	.notPrefetched
     28  7b7d
     29  7b7d		       29 7f		      and	#%01111111
     30  7b7f		       95 d2		      sta	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     31  7b81
     32  7b81		       2c f4 fb 	      bit	tt_Bit6Set
     33  7b84				   .notPrefetched
     34  7b84		       a8		      tay
     35  7b85					      ENDIF
     36  7b85		       b1 d8		      lda	(tt_ptr),y
     37  7b87
     38  7b87
     39  7b87
     40  7b87		       d0 06		      bne	.noEndOfPattern
     41  7b89
     42  7b89		       95 d2		      sta	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     43  7b8b		       f6 d0		      inc	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x
     44  7b8d		       d0 d1		      bne	.constructPatPtr
     45  7b8f				   .noEndOfPattern
    156  7b8f		       60		      rts
    157  7b90					      ENDIF
    158  7b90
    159  7b90
    160  7b90							; --- start instrument or percussion ---
    161  7b90				   .newNote
    162  7b90		       95 d6		      sta	tt_cur_ins_c0,x	; set new instrument
    163  7b92							; Instrument or percussion?
    164  7b92		       c9 20		      cmp	#TT_FREQ_MASK+1
    165  7b94		       b0 06		      bcs	.startInstrument
    166  7b96
    167  7b96							; --- start percussion ---
    168  7b96							; Get index of envelope
    169  7b96		       a8		      tay
    170  7b97							; -TT_FIRST_PERC because percussion start with TT_FIRST_PERC
    171  7b97		       b9 d0 fc 	      lda	tt_PercIndexes-TT_FIRST_PERC,y
    172  7b9a		       d0 08		      bne	.storeADIndex	; unconditional, since index values are >0
    173  7b9c
    174  7b9c							; --- start instrument ---
    175  7b9c				   .startInstrument
    176  7b9c					      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 1
    177  7b9c							; If V flag is set, this note had been pre-fetched. That means
    178  7b9c							; it should remain in sustain.
    179  7b9c		       70 08		      bvs	.finishedNewNote
    180  7b9e					      ENDIF
    181  7b9e							; Put note into attack/decay
    182  7b9e		       20 ee fb 	      jsr	tt_CalcInsIndex
    183  7ba1		       b9 a2 fc 	      lda	tt_InsADIndexes-1,y	; -1 because instruments start at #1
    184  7ba4				   .storeADIndex
    185  7ba4		       95 d4		      sta	tt_envelope_index_c0,x
    186  7ba6
    187  7ba6							; --- Finished parsing new note ---
    188  7ba6				   .finishedNewNote
    189  7ba6							; increase note index into pattern
    190  7ba6		       f6 d2		      inc	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
    191  7ba8							; loop over channels
    192  7ba8				   .sequencerNextChannel
    193  7ba8		       ca		      dex
    194  7ba9		       10 9f		      bpl	.advanceLoop
    195  7bab
    196  7bab							; Reset timer value
    197  7bab				  -	      IF	TT_GLOBAL_SPEED = 0
    198  7bab				  -			; Get timer value for current pattern in channel 0
    199  7bab				  -	      ldx	tt_cur_pat_index_c0	; get current pattern (index into tt_SequenceTable)
    200  7bab				  -	      ldy	tt_SequenceTable,x	; Current pattern index now in y
    201  7bab				  -	      IF	TT_USE_FUNKTEMPO = 0
    202  7bab				  -	      lda	tt_PatternSpeeds,y
    203  7bab				  -	      sta	tt_timer
    204  7bab				  -	      ELSE
    205  7bab				  -			; Test for odd/even frame
    206  7bab				  -	      lda	tt_cur_note_index_c0
    207  7bab				  -	      lsr
    208  7bab				  -	      lda	tt_PatternSpeeds,y	; does not affect carry flag
    209  7bab				  -	      bcc	.evenFrame
    210  7bab				  -	      and	#$0f	; does not affect carry flag
    211  7bab				  -	      bcs	.storeFunkTempo
    212  7bab				  -.evenFrame
    213  7bab				  -	      lsr
    214  7bab				  -	      lsr
    215  7bab				  -	      lsr
    216  7bab				  -	      lsr
    217  7bab				  -.storeFunkTempo
    218  7bab				  -	      sta	tt_timer
    219  7bab				  -	      ENDIF		; TT_USE_FUNKTEMPO = 0
    220  7bab				  -
    221  7bab					      ELSE
    222  7bab							; Global tempo
    223  7bab		       a2 04		      ldx	#TT_SPEED-1
    224  7bad					      IF	TT_USE_FUNKTEMPO = 1
    225  7bad		       a5 d2		      lda	tt_cur_note_index_c0
    226  7baf		       4a		      lsr
    227  7bb0		       90 02		      bcc	.noOddFrame
    228  7bb2		       a2 03		      ldx	#TT_ODD_SPEED-1
    229  7bb4				   .noOddFrame
    230  7bb4					      ENDIF		; TT_USE_FUNKTEMPO = 1
    231  7bb4		       86 cf		      stx	tt_timer
    232  7bb6					      ENDIF		; TT_GLOBAL_SPEED = 0
    233  7bb6
    234  7bb6							; No new note to process
    235  7bb6				   .noNewNote
    236  7bb6
    237  7bb6							; ==================== Update registers ====================
    238  7bb6		       a2 01		      ldx	#1	; 2 channels
    239  7bb8				   .updateLoop
    240  7bb8							; Percussion or melodic instrument?
    241  7bb8		       b5 d6		      lda	tt_cur_ins_c0,x
    242  7bba				  -	      IF	TT_STARTS_WITH_NOTES = 0
    243  7bba				  -			; This branch can be removed if track starts with a note in each channel
    244  7bba				  -	      beq	.afterAudioUpdate
    245  7bba					      ENDIF
    246  7bba		       c9 20		      cmp	#TT_FREQ_MASK+1
    247  7bbc		       b0 37		      bcs	.instrument	; Melodic instrument
    248  7bbe
    249  7bbe							; --- Percussion: Get envelope index ---
    250  7bbe		       b4 d4		      ldy	tt_envelope_index_c0,x
    251  7bc0							; Set AUDC and AUDV value from envelope
    252  7bc0		       b9 f9 fc 	      lda	tt_PercCtrlVolTable-1,y	; -1 because values are stored +1
    253  7bc3		       f0 02		      beq	.endOfPercussion	; 0 means end of percussion data
    254  7bc5		       f6 d4		      inc	tt_envelope_index_c0,x	; if end not reached: advance index
    255  7bc7				   .endOfPercussion
    256  7bc7		       95 59		      sta	AUDV0,x
    257  7bc9		       4a		      lsr
    258  7bca		       4a		      lsr
    259  7bcb		       4a		      lsr
    260  7bcc		       4a		      lsr
    261  7bcd		       95 55		      sta	AUDC0,x
    262  7bcf							; Set AUDF
    263  7bcf		       b9 e3 fc 	      lda	tt_PercFreqTable-1,y	; -1 because values are stored +1
    264  7bd2							; Bit 7 (overlay) might be set, but is unused in AUDF
    265  7bd2		       95 57		      sta	AUDF0,x
    266  7bd4					      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 1
    267  7bd4		       10 48		      bpl	.afterAudioUpdate
    268  7bd6							; Overlay percussion: Fetch next note out of order
    269  7bd6		       20 60 fb 	      jsr	tt_FetchNote
    270  7bd9							; Only do something if it's a melodic instrument
    271  7bd9		       c9 20		      cmp	#TT_FREQ_MASK+1
    272  7bdb		       90 41		      bcc	.afterAudioUpdate
    273  7bdd							; Instrument: Put into sustain
    274  7bdd		       95 d6		      sta	tt_cur_ins_c0,x	; set new instrument
    275  7bdf		       20 ee fb 	      jsr	tt_CalcInsIndex
    276  7be2		       b9 a7 fc 	      lda	tt_InsSustainIndexes-1,y	; -1 because instruments start at #1
    277  7be5		       95 d4		      sta	tt_envelope_index_c0,x
    278  7be7							; Set prefetch flag. asl-sec-ror is smaller than lda-ora #128-sta
    279  7be7		       16 d2		      asl	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
    280  7be9		       38		      sec
    281  7bea		       76 d2		      ror	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
    282  7bec		       30 30		      bmi	.afterAudioUpdate	; unconditional
    283  7bee				  -	      ELSE
    284  7bee				  -	      jmp	.afterAudioUpdate
    285  7bee					      ENDIF
    286  7bee
    287  7bee
    288  7bee							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    289  7bee							; Helper subroutine to minimize ROM footprint.
    290  7bee							; Interleaved here so player routine can be inlined.
    291  7bee							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    292  7bee				   tt_CalcInsIndex
    293  7bee							; move upper 3 bits to lower 3
    294  7bee		       4a		      lsr
    295  7bef		       4a		      lsr
    296  7bf0		       4a		      lsr
    297  7bf1		       4a		      lsr
    298  7bf2		       4a		      lsr
    299  7bf3		       a8		      tay
    300  7bf4				   tt_Bit6Set		; This opcode has bit #6 set, for use with bit instruction
    301  7bf4		       60		      rts
    302  7bf5
    303  7bf5
    304  7bf5				   .instrument
    305  7bf5							; --- Melodic instrument ---
    306  7bf5							; Compute index into ADSR indexes and master Ctrl tables
    307  7bf5		       20 ee fb 	      jsr	tt_CalcInsIndex
    308  7bf8							; Set AUDC with master value for this instrument, while we are at it
    309  7bf8		       b9 9d fc 	      lda	tt_InsCtrlTable-1,y	; -1 because instruments start with #1
    310  7bfb		       95 55		      sta	AUDC0,x
    311  7bfd							; advance ADSR counter and compare to end of Sustain
    312  7bfd		       b5 d4		      lda	tt_envelope_index_c0,x
    313  7bff		       d9 ac fc 	      cmp	tt_InsReleaseIndexes-1,y	; -1 because instruments start with #1
    314  7c02		       d0 03		      bne	.noEndOfSustain
    315  7c04							; End of sustain: Go back to start of sustain
    316  7c04		       b9 a7 fc 	      lda	tt_InsSustainIndexes-1,y	; -1 because instruments start with #1
    317  7c07				   .noEndOfSustain
    318  7c07		       a8		      tay
    319  7c08							; Set volume from envelope
    320  7c08		       b9 b2 fc 	      lda	tt_InsFreqVolTable,y
    321  7c0b		       f0 01		      beq	.endOfEnvelope	; 0 means end of release has been reached:
    322  7c0d		       c8		      iny		; advance index otherwise
    323  7c0e				   .endOfEnvelope
    324  7c0e		       94 d4		      sty	tt_envelope_index_c0,x
    325  7c10		       95 59		      sta	AUDV0,x
    326  7c12							; Now adjust frequency with ADSR value from envelope
    327  7c12		       4a		      lsr
    328  7c13		       4a		      lsr
    329  7c14		       4a		      lsr
    330  7c15		       4a		      lsr
    331  7c16		       18		      clc
    332  7c17		       75 d6		      adc	tt_cur_ins_c0,x
    333  7c19		       38		      sec
    334  7c1a		       e9 08		      sbc	#8
    335  7c1c		       95 57		      sta	AUDF0,x
    336  7c1e
    337  7c1e				   .afterAudioUpdate
    338  7c1e							; loop over channels
    339  7c1e		       ca		      dex
    340  7c1f		       10 97		      bpl	.updateLoop
    341  7c21
 Music player size:  $dd

     16  7c9e							; limitations under the License.
     17  7c9e
     18  7c9e							; Song author: 
     19  7c9e							; Song name: 
     20  7c9e
     21  7c9e							; @com.wudsn.ide.asm.hardware=ATARI2600
     22  7c9e
     23  7c9e							; =====================================================================
     24  7c9e							; TIATracker melodic and percussion instruments, patterns and sequencer
     25  7c9e							; data.
     26  7c9e							; =====================================================================
     27  7c9e				   tt_TrackDataStart
     28  7c9e
     29  7c9e							; =====================================================================
     30  7c9e							; Melodic instrument definitions (up to 7). tt_envelope_index_c0/1 hold
     31  7c9e							; the index values into these tables for the current instruments played
     32  7c9e							; in channel 0 and 1.
     33  7c9e							; 
     34  7c9e							; Each instrument is defined by:
     35  7c9e							; - tt_InsCtrlTable: the AUDC value
     36  7c9e							; - tt_InsADIndexes: the index of the start of the ADSR envelope as
     37  7c9e							;	 defined in tt_InsFreqVolTable
     38  7c9e							; - tt_InsSustainIndexes: the index of the start of the Sustain phase
     39  7c9e							;	 of the envelope
     40  7c9e							; - tt_InsReleaseIndexes: the index of the start of the Release phase
     41  7c9e							; - tt_InsFreqVolTable: The AUDF frequency and AUDV volume values of
     42  7c9e							;	 the envelope
     43  7c9e							; =====================================================================
     44  7c9e
     45  7c9e							; Instrument master CTRL values
     46  7c9e				   tt_InsCtrlTable
     47  7c9e		       07 04 0c 04*	      dc.b	$07, $04, $0c, $04, $0c
     48  7ca3
     49  7ca3
     50  7ca3							; Instrument Attack/Decay start indexes into ADSR tables.
     51  7ca3				   tt_InsADIndexes
     52  7ca3		       00 0e 0e 1e*	      dc.b	$00, $0e, $0e, $1e, $1e
     53  7ca8
     54  7ca8
     55  7ca8							; Instrument Sustain start indexes into ADSR tables
     56  7ca8				   tt_InsSustainIndexes
     57  7ca8		       08 19 19 2b*	      dc.b	$08, $19, $19, $2b, $2b
     58  7cad
     59  7cad
     60  7cad							; Instrument Release start indexes into ADSR tables
     61  7cad							; Caution: Values are stored with an implicit -1 modifier! To get the
     62  7cad							; real index, add 1.
     63  7cad				   tt_InsReleaseIndexes
     64  7cad		       09 1b 1b 2c*	      dc.b	$09, $1b, $1b, $2c, $2c
     65  7cb2
     66  7cb2
     67  7cb2							; AUDVx and AUDFx ADSR envelope values.
     68  7cb2							; Each byte encodes the frequency and volume:
     69  7cb2							; - Bits 7..4: Freqency modifier for the current note ([-8..7]),
     70  7cb2							;	 8 means no change. Bit 7 is the sign bit.
     71  7cb2							; - Bits 3..0: Volume
     72  7cb2							; Between sustain and release is one byte that is not used and
     73  7cb2							; can be any value.
     74  7cb2							; The end of the release phase is encoded by a 0.
     75  7cb2				   tt_InsFreqVolTable
     76  7cb2							; 0: Pizzicato bassb
     77  7cb2		       8a 8a 89 88*	      dc.b	$8a, $8a, $89, $88, $86, $85, $85, $84
     78  7cba		       83 00 83 83*	      dc.b	$83, $00, $83, $83, $83, $00
     79  7cc0							; 1+2: Square2
     80  7cc0		       8c 8c 8b 89*	      dc.b	$8c, $8c, $8b, $89, $87, $85, $84, $83
     81  7cc8		       82 82 81 81*	      dc.b	$82, $82, $81, $81, $81, $00, $81, $00
     82  7cd0							; 3+4: Square
     83  7cd0		       85 85 85 85*	      dc.b	$85, $85, $85, $85, $84, $83, $83, $82
     84  7cd8		       82 82 81 81*	      dc.b	$82, $82, $81, $81, $81, $81, $00, $80
     85  7ce0		       00		      dc.b	$00
     86  7ce1
     87  7ce1
     88  7ce1
     89  7ce1							; =====================================================================
     90  7ce1							; Percussion instrument definitions (up to 15)
     91  7ce1							;
     92  7ce1							; Each percussion instrument is defined by:
     93  7ce1							; - tt_PercIndexes: The index of the first percussion frame as defined
     94  7ce1							;	 in tt_PercFreqTable and tt_PercCtrlVolTable
     95  7ce1							; - tt_PercFreqTable: The AUDF frequency value
     96  7ce1							; - tt_PercCtrlVolTable: The AUDV volume and AUDC values
     97  7ce1							; =====================================================================
     98  7ce1
     99  7ce1							; Indexes into percussion definitions signifying the first frame for
    100  7ce1							; each percussion in tt_PercFreqTable.
    101  7ce1							; Caution: Values are stored with an implicit +1 modifier! To get the
    102  7ce1							; real index, subtract 1.
    103  7ce1				   tt_PercIndexes
    104  7ce1		       01 0a 0c 	      dc.b	$01, $0a, $0c
    105  7ce4
    106  7ce4
    107  7ce4							; The AUDF frequency values for the percussion instruments.
    108  7ce4							; If the second to last value is negative (>=128), it means it's an
    109  7ce4							; "overlay" percussion, i.e. the player fetches the next instrument note
    110  7ce4							; immediately and starts it in the sustain phase next frame. (Needs
    111  7ce4							; TT_USE_OVERLAY)
    112  7ce4				   tt_PercFreqTable
    113  7ce4							; 0: Kick
    114  7ce4		       00 01 02 03*	      dc.b	$00, $01, $02, $03, $04, $05, $06, $87
    115  7cec		       00		      dc.b	$00
    116  7ced							; 1: HH
    117  7ced		       80 00		      dc.b	$80, $00
    118  7cef							; 2: Snare
    119  7cef		       01 03 06 0e*	      dc.b	$01, $03, $06, $0e, $13, $11, $15, $14
    120  7cf7		       17 1b 00 	      dc.b	$17, $1b, $00
    121  7cfa
    122  7cfa
    123  7cfa							; The AUDCx and AUDVx volume values for the percussion instruments.
    124  7cfa							; - Bits 7..4: AUDC value
    125  7cfa							; - Bits 3..0: AUDV value
    126  7cfa							; 0 means end of percussion data.
    127  7cfa				   tt_PercCtrlVolTable
    128  7cfa							; 0: Kick
    129  7cfa		       ee ed ed eb*	      dc.b	$ee, $ed, $ed, $eb, $e9, $e8, $e8, $e6
    130  7d02		       00		      dc.b	$00
    131  7d03							; 1: HH
    132  7d03		       87 00		      dc.b	$87, $00
    133  7d05							; 2: Snare
    134  7d05		       8b 8a 8a 8a*	      dc.b	$8b, $8a, $8a, $8a, $8a, $8a, $89, $88
    135  7d0d		       87 86 00 	      dc.b	$87, $86, $00
    136  7d10
    137  7d10
    138  7d10
    139  7d10							; =====================================================================
    140  7d10							; Track definition
    141  7d10							; The track is defined by:
    142  7d10							; - tt_PatternX (X=0, 1, ...): Pattern definitions
    143  7d10							; - tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi: Pointers to the tt_PatternX tables, serving
    144  7d10							;	 as index values
    145  7d10							; - tt_SequenceTable: The order in which the patterns should be played,
    146  7d10							;	 i.e. indexes into tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi. Contains the sequences
    147  7d10							;	 for all channels and sub-tracks. The variables
    148  7d10							;	 tt_cur_pat_index_c0/1 hold an index into tt_SequenceTable for
    149  7d10							;	 each channel.
    150  7d10							;
    151  7d10							; So tt_SequenceTable holds indexes into tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi, which
    152  7d10							; in turn point to pattern definitions (tt_PatternX) in which the notes
    153  7d10							; to play are specified.
    154  7d10							; =====================================================================
    155  7d10
    156  7d10							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    157  7d10							; Pattern definitions, one table per pattern. tt_cur_note_index_c0/1
    158  7d10							; hold the index values into these tables for the current pattern
    159  7d10							; played in channel 0 and 1.
    160  7d10							;
    161  7d10							; A pattern is a sequence of notes (one byte per note) ending with a 0.
    162  7d10							; A note can be either:
    163  7d10							; - Pause: Put melodic instrument into release. Must only follow a
    164  7d10							;	 melodic instrument.
    165  7d10							; - Hold: Continue to play last note (or silence). Default "empty" note.
    166  7d10							; - Slide (needs TT_USE_SLIDE): Adjust frequency of last melodic note
    167  7d10							;	 by -7..+7 and keep playing it
    168  7d10							; - Play new note with melodic instrument
    169  7d10							; - Play new note with percussion instrument
    170  7d10							; - End of pattern
    171  7d10							;
    172  7d10							; A note is defined by:
    173  7d10							; - Bits 7..5: 1-7 means play melodic instrument 1-7 with a new note
    174  7d10							;	 and frequency in bits 4..0. If bits 7..5 are 0, bits 4..0 are
    175  7d10							;	 defined as:
    176  7d10							;	 - 0: End of pattern
    177  7d10							;	 - [1..15]: Slide -7..+7 (needs TT_USE_SLIDE)
    178  7d10							;	 - 8: Hold
    179  7d10							;	 - 16: Pause
    180  7d10							;	 - [17..31]: Play percussion instrument 1..15
    181  7d10							;
    182  7d10							; The tracker must ensure that a pause only follows a melodic
    183  7d10							; instrument or a hold/slide.
    184  7d10							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    185  7d10		       00 1f	   TT_FREQ_MASK =	%00011111
    186  7d10		       00 08	   TT_INS_HOLD =	8
    187  7d10		       00 10	   TT_INS_PAUSE =	16
    188  7d10		       00 11	   TT_FIRST_PERC =	17
    189  7d10
    190  7d10							; Intro left
    191  7d10				   tt_pattern0
    192  7d10		       11 08 3e 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $3e, $08, $12, $3e, $3e, $08
    193  7d18		       13 08 3e 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $3e, $08, $12, $3e, $3e, $08
    194  7d20		       11 08 3e 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $3e, $08, $12, $3e, $12, $3e
    195  7d28		       13 08 3e 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $3e, $08, $12, $3e, $13, $08
    196  7d30		       00		      dc.b	$00
    197  7d31
    198  7d31							; Intro2 L
    199  7d31				   tt_pattern1
    200  7d31		       11 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $34, $08
    201  7d39		       13 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $34, $08
    202  7d41		       11 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $12, $34
    203  7d49		       13 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $13, $08
    204  7d51		       00		      dc.b	$00
    205  7d52
    206  7d52							; Intro2-fill L
    207  7d52				   tt_pattern2
    208  7d52		       11 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $34, $08
    209  7d5a		       13 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $34, $08
    210  7d62		       11 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $12, $34
    211  7d6a		       13 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $13, $08
    212  7d72		       00		      dc.b	$00
    213  7d73
    214  7d73							; Intro right
    215  7d73				   tt_pattern3
    216  7d73		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $6e, $08, $73, $08
    217  7d7b		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $73, $08, $73, $08
    218  7d83		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $6e, $08, $b3, $08
    219  7d8b		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $b3, $08, $73, $08
    220  7d93		       00		      dc.b	$00
    221  7d94
    222  7d94							; Intro2 R
    223  7d94				   tt_pattern4
    224  7d94		       71 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$71, $08, $73, $08, $74, $08, $71, $08
    225  7d9c		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $b3, $08, $73, $08
    226  7da4		       b3 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$b3, $08, $73, $08, $b3, $08, $73, $08
    227  7dac		       71 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$71, $08, $73, $08, $74, $08, $71, $08
    228  7db4		       00		      dc.b	$00
    229  7db5
    230  7db5
    231  7db5
    232  7db5
    233  7db5							; Individual pattern speeds (needs TT_GLOBAL_SPEED = 0).
    234  7db5							; Each byte encodes the speed of one pattern in the order
    235  7db5							; of the tt_PatternPtr tables below.
    236  7db5							; If TT_USE_FUNKTEMPO is 1, then the low nibble encodes
    237  7db5							; the even speed and the high nibble the odd speed.
    238  7db5				  -	      IF	TT_GLOBAL_SPEED = 0
    239  7db5				  -tt_PatternSpeeds
    240  7db5				  -%%PATTERNSPEEDS%%
    241  7db5					      ENDIF
    242  7db5
    243  7db5
    244  7db5							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    245  7db5							; Pattern pointers look-up table.
    246  7db5							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    247  7db5				   tt_PatternPtrLo
    248  7db5		       10 31 52 73	      dc.b	<tt_pattern0, <tt_pattern1, <tt_pattern2, <tt_pattern3
    249  7db9		       94		      dc.b	<tt_pattern4
    250  7dba				   tt_PatternPtrHi
    251  7dba		       fd fd fd fd	      dc.b	>tt_pattern0, >tt_pattern1, >tt_pattern2, >tt_pattern3
    252  7dbe		       fd		      dc.b	>tt_pattern4
    253  7dbf
    254  7dbf
    255  7dbf							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    256  7dbf							; Pattern sequence table. Each byte is an index into the
    257  7dbf							; tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi tables where the pointers to the pattern
    258  7dbf							; definitions can be found. When a pattern has been played completely,
    259  7dbf							; the next byte from this table is used to get the address of the next
    260  7dbf							; pattern to play. tt_cur_pat_index_c0/1 hold the current index values
    261  7dbf							; into this table for channels 0 and 1.
    262  7dbf							; If TT_USE_GOTO is used, a value >=128 denotes a goto to the pattern
    263  7dbf							; number encoded in bits 6..0 (i.e. value AND %01111111).
    264  7dbf							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    265  7dbf				   tt_SequenceTable
    266  7dbf							; ---------- Channel 0 ----------
    267  7dbf		       00 00 01 02*	      dc.b	$00, $00, $01, $02, $80
    268  7dc4
    269  7dc4
    270  7dc4							; ---------- Channel 1 ----------
    271  7dc4		       03 04 03 04*	      dc.b	$03, $04, $03, $04, $85
    272  7dc9
    273  7dc9
 Track size:  $12b
    274  7dc9					      echo	"Track size: ", *-tt_TrackDataStart
